[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/lib/test-questions.ts
  contents: /**
 * 知己 · 四大核心性格测试题库
 * 包含：MBTI(28题)、PDP(30题)、DISC(24题)、盖洛普优势(20题)
 * 数据来源：参考国际标准测评框架，优化为中文快测版本
 */

// ============================================================
// 通用类型定义
// ============================================================

/** 单道测试题 */
export interface TestQuestion {
  id: number
  question: string
  options: TestOption[]
}

/** 测试选项 */
export interface TestOption {
  label: string
  value: string
  score?: number // PDP/DISC 用评分制
}

/** 测试配置 */
export interface TestConfig {
  id: string
  title: string
  subtitle: string
  description: string
  icon: string // lucide 图标名
  color: string // tailwind 渐变色
  questionCount: number
  estimatedTime: string // 预估时间
  questions: TestQuestion[]
  calculateResult: (answers: Record<number, string | number>) => TestResult
}

/** 测试结果 */
export interface TestResult {
  type: string // 结果类型标识
  typeName: string // 类型中文名
  summary: string // 简短总结
  sections: {
    heading: string
    content: string
    highlight?: boolean
  }[]
  scores?: Record<string, number> // 各维度得分
}

// ============================================================

// ============================================================

/** 计算 MBTI 结果 */
function calculateMBTI(answers: Record<number, string | number>): TestResult {
  let e = 0, i = 0, s = 0, n = 0, t = 0, f = 0, j = 0, p = 0

  Object.values(answers).forEach((v) => {
    const val = String(v)
    if (val === "E") e++
    if (val === "I") i++
    if (val === "S") s++
    if (val === "N") n++
    if (val === "T") t++
    if (val === "F") f++
    if (val === "J") j++
    if (val === "P") p++
  })

  const type = `${e >= i ? "E" : "I"}${s >= n ? "S" : "N"}${t >= f ? "T" : "F"}${j >= p ? "J" : "P"}`
  const detail = mbtiTypeDetails[type] || { name: "未知", title: "", desc: "", strengths: "", careers: "" }

  return {
    type,
    typeName: `${type} - ${detail.name}`,
    summary: detail.title,
    sections: [
      { heading: `${type} · ${detail.name}`, content: detail.desc, highlight: true },
      { heading: "维度得分", content: `外向E(${e}) / 内向I(${i}) · 实感S(${s}) / 直觉N(${n}) · 思考T(${t}) / 情感F(${f}) · 判断J(${j}) / 感知P(${p})` },
      { heading: "核心优势", content: detail.strengths },
      { heading: "推荐职业", content: detail.careers },
      { heading: "成长建议", content: type.startsWith("I") ? "适当增加社交互动，练习快速表达想法" : "学会独处反思，培养深度思考能力" },
    ],
    scores: { E: e, I: i, S: s, N: n, T: t, F: f, J: j, P: p },
  }
}

/** PDP 题目与类型对应关系（老虎/考拉/孔雀/猫头鹰/变色龙） */
const pdpTypeMap: Record<string, number[]> = {
  tiger: [1, 6, 11, 16, 21, 26],     // 老虎型
  koala: [2, 7, 12, 17, 22, 27],      // 考拉型
  peacock: [3, 8, 13, 18, 23, 28],    // 孔雀型
  owl: [4, 9, 14, 19, 24, 29],        // 猫头鹰型
  chameleon: [5, 10, 15, 20, 25, 30], // 变色龙型
}

const pdpTypeInfo: Record<string, { name: string; animal: string; desc: string; strengths: string; weaknesses: string; careers: string }> = {
  tiger: { name: "老虎型", animal: "🐯", desc: "成果导向的支配型人格。果断、勇敢、有竞争力，天生领导者", strengths: "目标明确 | 果断高效 | 敢于冒险 | 领导力强", weaknesses: "可能过于强势，忽略他人感受", careers: "企业管理 | 创业者 | 销售总监 | 项目经理" },
  koala: { name: "考拉型", animal: "🐨", desc: "价值导向的耐心型人格。温和、稳健、忠诚、重感情", strengths: "耐心温和 | 忠诚可靠 | 善于倾听 | 团队协作", weaknesses: "可能过于保守，缺乏主动性", careers: "人力资源 | 客服管理 | 教师 | 社工" },
  peacock: { name: "孔雀型", animal: "🦚", desc: "人际导向的表达型人格。外向、活泼、富有感染力和创造力", strengths: "表达能力 | 感染力强 | 创意丰富 | 社交达人", weaknesses: "可能过于情绪化，注意力分散", careers: "市场营销 | 公关 | 培训师 | 主持人" },
  owl: { name: "猫头鹰型", animal: "🦉", desc: "过程导向的精确型人格。严谨、细致、注重数据和逻辑", strengths: "分析能力 | 严谨细致 | 逻辑清晰 | 追求完美", weaknesses: "可能过于纠结细节，决策较慢", careers: "数据分析 | 财务审计 | 质量管理 | 研究员" },
  chameleon: { name: "变色龙型", animal: "🦎", desc: "组织导向的协调型人格。适应力强，善于协调各方关系", strengths: "适应力强 | 协调能力 | 灵活变通 | 人际敏感", weaknesses: "可能缺乏主见，过于迎合他人", careers: "项目协调 | 行政管理 | 外交 | 咨询顾问" },
}

/** 计算 PDP 结果 */
function calculatePDP(answers: Record<number, string | number>): TestResult {
  const scores: Record<string, number> = { tiger: 0, koala: 0, peacock: 0, owl: 0, chameleon: 0 }

  Object.entries(pdpTypeMap).forEach(([type, questionIds]) => {
    questionIds.forEach((qId) => {
      scores[type] += Number(answers[qId] || 0)
    })
  })

  const sorted = Object.entries(scores).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
  const primaryType = sorted[0][0]
  const secondaryType = sorted[1][0]
  const info = pdpTypeInfo[primaryType]
  const secondInfo = pdpTypeInfo[secondaryType]

  return {
    type: primaryType,
    typeName: `${info.name} ${info.animal}`,
    summary: info.desc,
    sections: [
      { heading: `主要类型：${info.name} ${info.animal}`, content: info.desc, highlight: true },
      { heading: "各类型得分", content: sorted.map(([k, v]) => `${pdpTypeInfo[k].animal}${pdpTypeInfo[k].name}：${v}分`).join(" | ") },
      { heading: "核心优势", content: info.strengths },
      { heading: `辅助类型：${secondInfo.name}`, content: `兼具${secondInfo.name}特质：${secondInfo.strengths.split(" | ").slice(0, 2).join("、")}` },
      { heading: "需要注意", content: info.weaknesses },
      { heading: "推荐职业", content: info.careers },
    ],
    scores: Object.fromEntries(sorted.map(([k, v]) => [pdpTypeInfo[k].name, v])),
  }
}

const discTypeInfo: Record<string, { name: string; fullName: string; desc: string; strengths: string; weaknesses: string; style: string; careers: string }> = {
  D: { name: "D型 · 支配型", fullName: "Dominance", desc: "结果导向的行动派。喜欢掌控、追求效率、果断决策", strengths: "领导力 | 果断高效 | 目标导向 | 抗压力强", weaknesses: "可能过于强势、缺乏耐心、忽略细节", style: "直接、简洁、注重结果", careers: "CEO | 创业者 | 项目经理 | 销售总监" },
  I: { name: "I型 · 影响型", fullName: "Influence", desc: "人际导向的社交家。热情、乐观、善于说服和感染他人", strengths: "社交能力 | 说服力 | 创造力 | 团队激励", weaknesses: "可能过于情绪化、缺乏细节关注、易分心", style: "热情、开放、富有感染力", careers: "市场营销 | 公关 | 培训师 | 销售" },
  S: { name: "S型 · 稳健型", fullName: "Steadiness", desc: "稳定导向的和平者。耐心、可靠、善于倾听和支持他人", strengths: "耐心可靠 | 善于倾听 | 团队协作 | 执行力强", weaknesses: "可能过于保守、不善拒绝、害怕变化", style: "温和、稳重、注重和谐", careers: "人力资源 | 客服 | 行政管理 | 教师" },
  C: { name: "C型 · 谨慎型", fullName: "Compliance", desc: "质量导向的完美者。严谨、细致、注重数据和标准", strengths: "分析能力 | 严谨细致 | 追求完美 | 逻辑清晰", weaknesses: "可能过于纠结细节、决策较慢、自我批评", style: "精确、系统、注重标准", careers: "财务分析 | 质量管理 | 数据分析 | 研究员" },
}

/** 计算 DISC 结果 */
function calculateDISC(answers: Record<number, string | number>): TestResult {
  const scores: Record<string, number> = { D: 0, I: 0, S: 0, C: 0 }

  Object.values(answers).forEach((v) => {
    const val = String(v)
    const type = val.charAt(0)  // D, I, S, C
    const score = parseInt(val.charAt(1)) || 0
    if (scores[type] !== undefined) {
      scores[type] += score
    }
  })

  const sorted = Object.entries(scores).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
  const primaryType = sorted[0][0]
  const secondaryType = sorted[1][0]
  const info = discTypeInfo[primaryType]

  return {
    type: primaryType,
    typeName: info.name,
    summary: info.desc,
    sections: [
      { heading: `主导风格：${info.name}`, content: info.desc, highlight: true },
      { heading: "四维得分", content: sorted.map(([k, v]) => `${discTypeInfo[k].name.split("·")[0].trim()}(${v}分)`).join(" | ") },
      { heading: "核心优势", content: info.strengths },
      { heading: "沟通风格", content: info.style },
      { heading: `辅助风格：${discTypeInfo[secondaryType].name}`, content: `兼具${discTypeInfo[secondaryType].fullName}特质` },
      { heading: "需要注意", content: info.weaknesses },
      { heading: "推荐职业", content: info.careers },
    ],
    scores: Object.fromEntries(sorted),
  }
}

/** 盖洛普四大领域 */
const gallupDomains: Record<string, { name: string; themes: string[]; desc: string }> = {
  executing: { name: "执行力", themes: ["成就", "专注", "责任", "统筹", "纪律"], desc: "你擅长将想法变为现实，是团队中的执行引擎" },
  influencing: { name: "影响力", themes: ["沟通", "追求", "自信", "竞争", "个别"], desc: "你善于影响他人，是天生的说服者和推动者" },
  relationship: { name: "关系建立", themes: ["交往", "和谐", "信仰", "体谅", "伯乐"], desc: "你擅长建立深度关系，是团队的黏合剂" },
  strategic: { name: "战略思维", themes: ["战略", "思维", "学习", "搜集", "回顾"], desc: "你擅长分析和规划，是团队的智囊" },
}

/** 计算盖洛普结果 */
function calculateGallup(answers: Record<number, string | number>): TestResult {
  const selectedThemes: string[] = []
  const domainScores: Record<string, number> = { executing: 0, influencing: 0, relationship: 0, strategic: 0 }

  Object.values(answers).forEach((v) => {
    const val = String(v)
    if (val !== "_") {
      selectedThemes.push(val)
      // 计算领域得分
      Object.entries(gallupDomains).forEach(([domain, info]) => {
        if (info.themes.includes(val)) {
          domainScores[domain]++
        }
      })
    }
  })

  const sortedDomains = Object.entries(domainScores).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
  const primaryDomain = sortedDomains[0][0]
  const domainInfo = gallupDomains[primaryDomain]
  const top5 = selectedThemes.slice(0, 5)

  return {
    type: primaryDomain,
    typeName: `${domainInfo.name}型`,
    summary: domainInfo.desc,
    sections: [
      { heading: `TOP5 天赋主题`, content: top5.length > 0 ? top5.join(" | ") : "战略 | 学习 | 思维 | 成就 | 沟通", highlight: true },
      { heading: "优势领域分布", content: sortedDomains.map(([k, v]) => `${gallupDomains[k].name}(${v})`).join(" | ") },
      { heading: `主导领域：${domainInfo.name}`, content: domainInfo.desc },
      { heading: "发展建议", content: "将天赋与技能相结合，在优势领域持续投入，让天赋成为真正的优势" },
      { heading: "团队角色", content: primaryDomain === "executing" ? "适合担任执行推动角色" : primaryDomain === "influencing" ? "适合担任营销说服角色" : primaryDomain === "relationship" ? "适合担任团队凝聚角色" : "适合担任决策顾问角色" },
    ],
    scores: Object.fromEntries(sortedDomains.map(([k, v]) => [gallupDomains[k].name, v])),
  }
}

 * 支持：测试列表、答题流程、结果展示、保存报告

import { useState } from "react"
import {
  Brain, Target, Award, ArrowLeft, ArrowRight, CheckCircle2,
  Loader2, Download, Share2, Clock, FileText, Sparkles, ChevronRight,
} from "lucide-react"
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button"
import { Card } from "@/components/ui/card"
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge"
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
import { testConfigs, type TestConfig, type TestResult } from "@/lib/test-questions"
import { reportDB } from "@/lib/local-db"

// 图标映射
const iconMap: Record<string, React.ElementType> = {
  Brain, Target, Award,
  Paw: Brain, // PDP 暂用 Brain 图标替代
}

interface TestPageProps {
  user: { id: string; name?: string; nickname?: string } | null
}

// 测试状态类型
type TestState = "list" | "intro" | "testing" | "loading" | "result"

export function TestPage({ user }: TestPageProps) {
  // 当前选中的测试
  const [selectedTest, setSelectedTest] = useState<TestConfig | null>(null)
  // 测试流程状态
  const [testState, setTestState] = useState<TestState>("list")
  // 当前题目索引
  const [currentQuestion, setCurrentQuestion] = useState(0)
  // 用户答案
  const [answers, setAnswers] = useState<Record<number, string | number>>({})
  // 测试结果
  const [result, setResult] = useState<TestResult | null>(null)
  // 保存状态
  const [saved, setSaved] = useState(false)

  /** 选择一个测试 */
  const handleSelectTest = (testId: string) => {
    const config = testConfigs[testId]
    if (config) {
      setSelectedTest(config)
      setTestState("intro")
      setCurrentQuestion(0)
      setAnswers({})
      setResult(null)
      setSaved(false)
    }
  }

  /** 开始测试 */
  const handleStartTest = () => {
    setTestState("testing")
    setCurrentQuestion(0)
  }

  /** 回答问题 */
  const handleAnswer = (questionId: number, value: string | number) => {
    const newAnswers = { ...answers, [questionId]: value }
    setAnswers(newAnswers)

    if (selectedTest) {
      const currentIdx = selectedTest.questions.findIndex(q => q.id === questionId)
      if (currentIdx < selectedTest.questions.length - 1) {
        // 自动跳转下一题
        setTimeout(() => setCurrentQuestion(currentIdx + 1), 300)
      } else {
        // 最后一题，生成结果
        setTestState("loading")
        setTimeout(() => {
          const testResult = selectedTest.calculateResult(newAnswers)
          setResult(testResult)
          setTestState("result")
        }, 1500)
      }
    }
  }

  /** 上一题 */
  const handlePrevQuestion = () => {
    if (currentQuestion > 0) {
      setCurrentQuestion(prev => prev - 1)
    }
  }

  /** 保存报告 */
  const handleSaveReport = () => {
    if (result && selectedTest && user) {
      reportDB.save({
        userId: user.id,
        type: selectedTest.id,
        name: `${selectedTest.title} - ${result.typeName}`,
        birthDate: "",
        result: result,
      })
      setSaved(true)
    }
  }

  /** 返回列表 */
  const handleBackToList = () => {
    setSelectedTest(null)
    setTestState("list")
    setCurrentQuestion(0)
    setAnswers({})
    setResult(null)
    setSaved(false)
  }

  /** 重新测试 */
  const handleRetake = () => {
    setTestState("intro")
    setCurrentQuestion(0)
    setAnswers({})
    setResult(null)
    setSaved(false)
  }

  // ============ 渲染：测试列表 ============
  if (testState === "list") {
    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-12 pb-28 space-y-5">
        {/* 头部 */}
        <header>
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-foreground flex items-center gap-2">
            性格测评
            <Sparkles className="w-5 h-5 text-coral animate-pulse" />
          </h1>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1">选择测评工具，探索真实的自己</p>
        </header>

        {/* 测试卡片列表 */}
        <div className="space-y-3">
          {Object.values(testConfigs).map((test) => {
            const Icon = iconMap[test.icon] || Brain
            return (
              <Card
                key={test.id}
                className="glass p-4 rounded-2xl border-0 hover:shadow-lg transition-all cursor-pointer active:scale-[0.98]"
                onClick={() => handleSelectTest(test.id)}
              >
                <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
                  <div className={cn(
                    "w-14 h-14 rounded-2xl bg-gradient-to-br flex items-center justify-center shadow-lg shrink-0",
                    test.color
                  )}>
                    <Icon className="w-7 h-7 text-white" />
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-0.5">
                      <h3 className="font-bold text-foreground">{test.title}</h3>
                      <Badge className="bg-coral/10 text-coral border-0 text-[10px]">
                        {test.questionCount}题
                      </Badge>
                    </div>
                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1.5">{test.subtitle}</p>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
                      <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                        <Clock className="w-3 h-3" />
                        {test.estimatedTime}
                      </span>
                      <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                        <FileText className="w-3 h-3" />
                        AI生成报告
                      </span>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <ChevronRight className="w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
                </div>
              </Card>
            )
          })}
        </div>

        {/* 底部提示 */}
        <div className="text-center pt-2">
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">每种测评免费1次 · AI智能生成解读报告</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  // ============ 渲染：测试介绍页 ============
  if (testState === "intro" && selectedTest) {
    const Icon = iconMap[selectedTest.icon] || Brain
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-50 via-white to-amber-50">
        <header className="glass-strong px-4 py-3 safe-top sticky top-0 z-10">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <button
              onClick={handleBackToList}
              className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-muted flex items-center justify-center text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors"
            >
              <ArrowLeft className="w-5 h-5" />
            </button>
            <h1 className="font-bold text-foreground">{selectedTest.title}</h1>
          </div>
        </header>

        <div className="px-6 py-8 flex flex-col items-center">
          {/* 图标 */}
          <div className={cn(
            "w-24 h-24 rounded-3xl bg-gradient-to-br flex items-center justify-center shadow-xl mb-6",
            selectedTest.color
          )}>
            <Icon className="w-12 h-12 text-white" />
          </div>

          {/* 标题 */}
          <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-foreground mb-2">{selectedTest.title}</h2>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center mb-6">{selectedTest.description}</p>

          {/* 信息卡片 */}
          <Card className="glass p-4 rounded-2xl border-0 w-full mb-8">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-around">
              <div className="text-center">
                <div className="text-lg font-bold text-coral">{selectedTest.questionCount}</div>
                <div className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">总题数</div>
              </div>
              <div className="w-px h-8 bg-border" />
              <div className="text-center">
                <div className="text-lg font-bold text-orange">{selectedTest.estimatedTime}</div>
                <div className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">预计用时</div>
              </div>
              <div className="w-px h-8 bg-border" />
              <div className="text-center">
                <div className="text-lg font-bold text-gold">免费</div>
                <div className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">首次体验</div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </Card>

          {/* 注意事项 */}
          <div className="w-full space-y-2 mb-8">
            <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-foreground">答题须知</h3>
            <div className="space-y-1.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
              <p>• 请根据第一反应选择最接近自己的选项</p>
              <p>• 没有对错之分，真实回答才能获得准确结果</p>
              <p>• 答题过程中可以随时返回上一题修改</p>
              <p>• 完成答题后AI会自动生成专属解读报告</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* 开始按钮 */}
          <Button
            onClick={handleStartTest}
            className={cn(
              "w-full bg-gradient-to-r text-white rounded-xl py-6 text-base font-medium shadow-xl",
              selectedTest.color
            )}
          >
            开始测试
            <ArrowRight className="w-5 h-5 ml-2" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  // ============ 渲染：答题中 ============
  if (testState === "testing" && selectedTest) {
    const question = selectedTest.questions[currentQuestion]
    if (!question) return null

    const progress = ((currentQuestion + 1) / selectedTest.questions.length) * 100
    const answeredCount = Object.keys(answers).length

    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-50 via-white to-amber-50 flex flex-col">
        {/* 顶部 */}
        <header className="glass-strong px-4 py-3 safe-top sticky top-0 z-10">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <button
              onClick={() => {
                if (currentQuestion === 0) {
                  setTestState("intro")
                } else {
                  handlePrevQuestion()
                }
              }}
              className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-muted flex items-center justify-center text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors"
            >
              <ArrowLeft className="w-5 h-5" />
            </button>
            <div className="flex-1">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1.5">
                <span>{selectedTest.title}</span>
                <span>{currentQuestion + 1} / {selectedTest.questions.length}</span>
              </div>
              <div className="h-1.5 bg-muted rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                <div
                  className={cn("h-full bg-gradient-to-r transition-all duration-500 ease-out", selectedTest.color)}
                  style={{ width: `${progress}%` }}
                />
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </header>

        {/* 题目内容 */}
        <div className="flex-1 px-5 py-6 flex flex-col">
          <div className="flex-1">
            {/* 题号 */}
            <div className={cn(
              "inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-r text-white text-xs font-medium mb-4",
              selectedTest.color
            )}>
              <span>第 {currentQuestion + 1} 题</span>
            </div>

            {/* 题目 */}
            <h2 className="text-lg font-bold text-foreground mb-6 leading-relaxed">
              {question.question}
            </h2>

            {/* 选项 */}
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {question.options.map((option, idx) => {
                const isSelected = answers[question.id] === option.value
                return (
                  <button
                    key={idx}
                    onClick={() => handleAnswer(question.id, option.value)}
                    className={cn(
                      "w-full p-4 rounded-2xl text-left transition-all duration-200 border-2",
                      isSelected
                        ? "border-coral bg-coral/10 shadow-md scale-[1.01]"
                        : "border-transparent glass hover:bg-coral/5 hover:border-coral/20 active:scale-[0.98]",
                    )}
                  >
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                      <div className={cn(
                        "w-7 h-7 rounded-full border-2 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 transition-all",
                        isSelected ? "border-coral bg-coral" : "border-muted-foreground/30"
                      )}>
                        {isSelected && <CheckCircle2 className="w-4 h-4 text-white" />}
                      </div>
                      <span className={cn(
                        "text-sm leading-relaxed",
                        isSelected ? "text-foreground font-medium" : "text-foreground"
                      )}>
                        {option.label}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                  </button>
                )
              })}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* 底部导航 */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between pt-6">
            <button
              onClick={handlePrevQuestion}
              disabled={currentQuestion === 0}
              className={cn(
                "flex items-center gap-1 text-sm transition-colors",
                currentQuestion === 0 ? "text-muted-foreground/30" : "text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
              )}
            >
              <ArrowLeft className="w-4 h-4" />
              上一题
            </button>
            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
              已答 {answeredCount} / {selectedTest.questions.length} 题
            </span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  // ============ 渲染：加载中 ============
  if (testState === "loading" && selectedTest) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-50 via-white to-amber-50 flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-6">
        <div className={cn(
          "w-20 h-20 rounded-3xl bg-gradient-to-br flex items-center justify-center shadow-xl mb-6",
          selectedTest.color
        )}>
          <Loader2 className="w-10 h-10 text-white animate-spin" />
        </div>
        <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-foreground mb-2">正在生成解读报告</h2>
        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center">AI正在分析你的答题数据...</p>
        <div className="mt-6 flex gap-1.5">
          <span className="w-2.5 h-2.5 bg-coral rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: "0ms" }} />
          <span className="w-2.5 h-2.5 bg-orange rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: "150ms" }} />
          <span className="w-2.5 h-2.5 bg-gold rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: "300ms" }} />
        </div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  // ============ 渲染：测试结果 ============
  if (testState === "result" && selectedTest && result) {
    const Icon = iconMap[selectedTest.icon] || Brain
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-50 via-white to-amber-50">
        <header className="glass-strong px-4 py-3 safe-top sticky top-0 z-10">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <button
              onClick={handleBackToList}
              className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-muted flex items-center justify-center text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors"
            >
              <ArrowLeft className="w-5 h-5" />
            </button>
            <h1 className="font-bold text-foreground">测试结果</h1>
          </div>
        </header>

        <div className="px-4 py-4 space-y-4 pb-32">
          {/* 结果卡片 */}
          <Card className={cn(
            "p-6 rounded-2xl border-0 bg-gradient-to-br text-white shadow-xl",
            selectedTest.color
          )}>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-4 mb-4">
              <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-2xl bg-white/20 backdrop-blur flex items-center justify-center">
                <Icon className="w-8 h-8 text-white" />
              </div>
              <div>
                <p className="text-white/80 text-xs">{selectedTest.title}</p>
                <h2 className="text-xl font-bold">{result.typeName}</h2>
              </div>
            </div>
            <p className="text-white/90 text-sm leading-relaxed">{result.summary}</p>
          </Card>

          {/* 详细分析 */}
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {result.sections.map((section, idx) => (
              <Card
                key={idx}
                className={cn(
                  "p-4 rounded-xl border",
                  section.highlight
                    ? "bg-gradient-to-r from-coral/10 to-gold/10 border-coral/20"
                    : "glass border-border/50",
                )}
              >
                <h3 className="font-semibold text-foreground text-sm mb-1.5">{section.heading}</h3>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">{section.content}</p>
              </Card>
            ))}
          </div>

          {/* 维度得分图表（如果有） */}
          {result.scores && (
            <Card className="glass p-4 rounded-2xl border-0">
              <h3 className="font-semibold text-foreground text-sm mb-3">维度得分</h3>
              <div className="space-y-2.5">
                {Object.entries(result.scores).map(([key, value]) => {
                  const maxScore = selectedTest.id === "mbti" ? 7 : selectedTest.id === "pdp" ? 30 : selectedTest.id === "disc" ? 30 : 5
                  const percentage = Math.round((Number(value) / maxScore) * 100)
                  return (
                    <div key={key} className="flex items-center gap-3">
                      <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground w-16 text-right shrink-0">{key}</span>
                      <div className="flex-1 h-2 bg-muted rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                        <div
                          className={cn("h-full bg-gradient-to-r rounded-full transition-all duration-700", selectedTest.color)}
                          style={{ width: `${Math.min(percentage, 100)}%` }}
                        />
                      </div>
                      <span className="text-xs font-medium text-foreground w-8">{String(value)}</span>
                    </div>
                  )
                })}
              </div>
            </Card>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* 底部操作栏 */}
        <div className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 p-4 bg-gradient-to-t from-white via-white to-transparent">
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Button
              onClick={handleSaveReport}
              disabled={saved}
              className={cn(
                "flex-1 rounded-xl py-5",
                saved
                  ? "bg-green-500 text-white"
                  : "bg-gradient-to-r from-coral to-gold text-white"
              )}
            >
              {saved ? (
                <>
                  <CheckCircle2 className="w-4 h-4 mr-1" />
                  已保存
                </>
              ) : (
                <>
                  <Download className="w-4 h-4 mr-1" />
                  保存报告
                </>
              )}
            </Button>
            <Button
              variant="outline"
              onClick={handleRetake}
              className="rounded-xl py-5 border-coral/30 text-coral hover:bg-coral/10 bg-transparent"
            >
              重新测试
            </Button>
            <Button
              variant="outline"
              className="rounded-xl py-5 border-coral/30 text-coral hover:bg-coral/10 bg-transparent"
            >
              <Share2 className="w-4 h-4" />
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  return null
}

  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/lib/mongodb.ts
  contents: /**
 * 知己 · MongoDB 连接工具
 * 使用 Next.js API Routes 连接 MongoDB
 * 端口：27017（固定）
 */

import { MongoClient, Db, type MongoClientOptions } from "mongodb"

// MongoDB 连接配置
const MONGODB_URI = process.env.MONGODB_URI || "mongodb://localhost:27017"
const MONGODB_DB = process.env.MONGODB_DB || "zhiji"

// 全局变量缓存连接（开发环境防止热更新重复连接）
let cachedClient: MongoClient | null = null
let cachedDb: Db | null = null

/** 连接选项 */
const options: MongoClientOptions = {
  maxPoolSize: 10,
  serverSelectionTimeoutMS: 5000,
  socketTimeoutMS: 45000,
}

/**
 * 获取 MongoDB 数据库连接
 * @returns Promise<{ client: MongoClient, db: Db }>
 */
export async function connectToDatabase(): Promise<{ client: MongoClient; db: Db }> {
  // 如果已缓存，直接返回
  if (cachedClient && cachedDb) {
    return { client: cachedClient, db: cachedDb }
  }

  // 创建新连接
  const client = new MongoClient(MONGODB_URI, options)
  await client.connect()
  const db = client.db(MONGODB_DB)

  // 缓存连接
  cachedClient = client
  cachedDb = db

  console.log("[知己] MongoDB 连接成功:", MONGODB_DB)
  return { client, db }
}

/**
 * 获取指定集合
 * @param collectionName 集合名
 */
export async function getCollection(collectionName: string) {
  const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
  return db.collection(collectionName)
}

// ============================================================
// 集合名常量
// ============================================================

export const COLLECTIONS = {
  USERS: "users",           // 用户表
  REPORTS: "reports",       // 解读报告
  TEST_RECORDS: "test_records", // 测试记录
  APPOINTMENTS: "appointments", // 咨询预约
  CONSULTANTS: "consultants",   // 专家/咨询师
  SURVEYS: "surveys",       // 调研记录
  INVITATIONS: "invitations", // 邀请记录
} as const

// ============================================================
// 数据库初始化（创建索引等）
// ============================================================

/**
 * 初始化数据库索引
 * 首次启动时调用
 */
export async function initializeDatabase() {
  try {
    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()

    // 用户表索引
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.USERS).createIndex({ phone: 1 }, { unique: true, sparse: true })
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.USERS).createIndex({ openId: 1 }, { unique: true, sparse: true })
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.USERS).createIndex({ inviteCode: 1 }, { unique: true })

    // 报告表索引
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.REPORTS).createIndex({ userId: 1, createdAt: -1 })
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.REPORTS).createIndex({ type: 1 })

    // 测试记录索引
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.TEST_RECORDS).createIndex({ userId: 1, type: 1, createdAt: -1 })

    // 预约表索引
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.APPOINTMENTS).createIndex({ userId: 1, status: 1 })
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.APPOINTMENTS).createIndex({ consultantId: 1, date: 1 })

    console.log("[知己] 数据库索引初始化完成")
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[知己] 数据库初始化失败:", error)
  }
}


[Tool result] Write

assistant:
[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/app/api/test/route.ts
  contents: /**
 * 知己 · 测试记录 API
 * POST /api/test - 保存测试记录和报告
 * GET /api/test?userId=xxx - 获取用户测试记录
 */

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
import { connectToDatabase, COLLECTIONS } from "@/lib/mongodb"

/** POST: 保存测试记录 */
export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await request.json()
    const { userId, testType, answers, result } = body

    if (!userId || !testType || !result) {
      return NextResponse.json(
        { error: "缺少必要参数: userId, testType, result" },
        { status: 400 }
      )
    }

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()

    // 保存测试记录
    const testRecord = {
      userId,
      type: testType,
      answers: answers || {},
      result,
      createdAt: new Date(),
    }
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.TEST_RECORDS).insertOne(testRecord)

    // 同时保存为报告
    const report = {
      userId,
      type: testType,
      name: `${result.typeName || testType} 测试报告`,
      result,
      isFavorite: false,
      createdAt: new Date(),
    }
    const reportResult = await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.REPORTS).insertOne(report)

    return NextResponse.json({
      success: true,
      message: "测试记录已保存",
      reportId: reportResult.insertedId,
    })
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error("[知己API] 保存测试记录失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json(
      { error: "服务器错误", detail: error.message },
      { status: 500 }
    )
  }
}

/** GET: 获取测试记录 */
export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const userId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get("userId")

    if (!userId) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: "缺少 userId 参数" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    const records = await db
      .collection(COLLECTIONS.TEST_RECORDS)
      .find({ userId })
      .sort({ createdAt: -1 })
      .limit(50)
      .toArray()

    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, data: records })
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error("[知己API] 获取测试记录失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json(
      { error: "服务器错误", detail: error.message },
      { status: 500 }
    )
  }
}

 * 知己 · AI 分析 API
 * POST /api/analysis - 一键AI分析（上传材料/聊天记录/生日）
 * 支持：文本分析、聊天记录分析、综合性格分析

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
import { connectToDatabase, COLLECTIONS } from "@/lib/mongodb"

/** AI 分析提示词模板 */
const ANALYSIS_PROMPTS: Record<string, string> = {
  birthday: `你是一位专业的性格分析师。请根据用户的出生日期，从以下维度进行综合分析：
1. 生命数字分析（主命数、天赋数、流年数）
2. 性格特质概述
3. 核心优势与潜在挑战
4. 职业发展建议
5. 人际关系特点
6. 2026年运势展望
请用专业但通俗易懂的语言，生成1000-2000字的解读报告。`,

  chatlog: `你是一位专业的心理分析师和性格测评师。请根据用户提供的聊天记录/社交动态内容，从以下维度分析此人的性格特征：
1. MBTI 性格类型推测（并给出推测依据）
2. DISC 行为风格分析
3. PDP 动物性格分析
4. 沟通风格特点
5. 情感表达模式
6. 核心价值观
7. 成长建议
请用专业但通俗易懂的语言，生成1000-2000字的综合分析报告。`,

  comprehensive: `你是一位多维度性格分析专家。请综合用户提供的所有信息（基本信息、测试结果、聊天记录等），生成一份全面的性格画像报告：
1. 性格核心特质
2. MBTI/PDP/DISC 综合匹配分析
3. 优势与盲区
4. 职业方向建议
5. 人际关系指导
6. 个人成长路径
请用专业但通俗易懂的语言，生成1500-2000字的全息解读报告。`,
}

/** POST: AI 分析 */
export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await request.json()
    const { userId, analysisType, birthday, chatlog, materials, name } = body

    if (!analysisType) {
      return NextResponse.json(
        { error: "缺少 analysisType 参数" },
        { status: 400 }
      )
    }

    // 构建分析内容
    let userContent = ""
    if (name) userContent += `姓名：${name}\n`
    if (birthday) userContent += `出生日期：${birthday}\n`
    if (chatlog) userContent += `\n聊天记录/社交动态：\n${chatlog}\n`
    if (materials) userContent += `\n补充材料：\n${materials}\n`

    if (!userContent.trim()) {
      return NextResponse.json(
        { error: "请提供至少一项分析内容（生日/聊天记录/材料）" },
        { status: 400 }
      )
    }

    const systemPrompt = ANALYSIS_PROMPTS[analysisType] || ANALYSIS_PROMPTS.comprehensive

    // 调用 AI 服务（支持 OpenAI / Groq / 本地模拟）
    let analysisResult: string

    const aiApiKey = process.env.AI_API_KEY
    const aiBaseUrl = process.env.AI_BASE_URL || "https://api.groq.com/openai/v1"

    if (aiApiKey) {
      // 调用真实 AI API
      try {
        const aiResponse = await fetch(`${aiBaseUrl}/chat/completions`, {
          method: "POST",
          headers: {
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
            "Authorization": `Bearer ${aiApiKey}`,
          },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            model: process.env.AI_MODEL || "llama-3.3-70b-versatile",
            messages: [
              { role: "system", content: systemPrompt },
              { role: "user", content: userContent },
            ],
            temperature: 0.7,
            max_tokens: 4096,
          }),
        })

        if (aiResponse.ok) {
          const aiData = await aiResponse.json()
          analysisResult = aiData.choices?.[0]?.message?.content || "AI分析未返回结果"
        } else {
          console.warn("[知己API] AI API 调用失败，使用模拟数据")
          analysisResult = generateMockAnalysis(analysisType, name, birthday, chatlog)
        }
      } catch (aiError) {
        console.warn("[知己API] AI API 请求异常，使用模拟数据:", aiError)
        analysisResult = generateMockAnalysis(analysisType, name, birthday, chatlog)
      }
    } else {
      // 无 API Key，使用模拟数据
      analysisResult = generateMockAnalysis(analysisType, name, birthday, chatlog)
    }

    // 保存到数据库（如果有 userId）
    if (userId) {
      try {
        const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
        await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.REPORTS).insertOne({
          userId,
          type: `ai-${analysisType}`,
          name: `AI${analysisType === "birthday" ? "生日" : analysisType === "chatlog" ? "聊天记录" : "综合"}分析报告`,
          result: { content: analysisResult, analysisType, inputData: { name, birthday, hasChatlog: !!chatlog } },
          createdAt: new Date(),
        })
      } catch (dbError) {
        console.warn("[知己API] 保存报告到数据库失败（继续返回结果）:", dbError)
      }
    }

    return NextResponse.json({
      success: true,
      data: {
        content: analysisResult,
        analysisType,
        createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      },
    })
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error("[知己API] AI 分析失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json(
      { error: "服务器错误", detail: error.message },
      { status: 500 }
    )
  }
}

/**
 * 知己 · 主入口页面
 * 四Tab路由：测评(test) → AI对话(chat) → 专家(consultant) → 我的(profile)
 * 子页面：报告中心、发起人驾驶舱
 */

import { useState, useEffect } from "react"
import { BottomNav, type TabType } from "@/components/bottom-nav"
import { TestPage } from "@/components/test-page"
import { ChatPage } from "@/components/chat-page"
import { ProfilePage } from "@/components/profile-page"
import { ReportsPage } from "@/components/reports-page"
import { InvitePage } from "@/components/invite-page"
import { ConsultantPage } from "@/components/consultant-page"
import { userDB, type User } from "@/lib/local-db"

// 子页面类型
type SubPage = "reports" | "invite" | null

export default function App() {
  // 主Tab状态
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<TabType>("test")
  // 子页面状态
  const [subPage, setSubPage] = useState<SubPage>(null)
  // 当前用户
  const [currentUser, setCurrentUser] = useState<User>({
    id: "default_user",
    phone: "13800138000",
    password: "",
    nickname: "知己用户",
    avatar: "",
    vip: false,
    points: 100,
    inviteCode: "ZHIJI01",
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  })

  // 初始化：加载用户数据
  useEffect(() => {
    const user = userDB.getCurrentUser()
    if (user) {
      setCurrentUser(user)
    }
  }, [])

  // 退出登录
  const handleLogout = () => {
    userDB.logout()
    setCurrentUser({
      id: "default_user",
      phone: "13800138000",
      password: "",
      nickname: "知己用户",
      avatar: "",
      vip: false,
      points: 100,
      inviteCode: "ZHIJI01",
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    })
  }

  // ============ 子页面渲染 ============

  // 报告中心
  if (subPage === "reports") {
    return <ReportsPage user={currentUser} onBack={() => setSubPage(null)} />
  }

  // 发起人驾驶舱
  if (subPage === "invite") {
    return <InvitePage user={currentUser} onBack={() => setSubPage(null)} />
  }

  // ============ 主页面渲染 ============

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-50 via-white to-amber-50 relative overflow-hidden">
      {/* 背景装饰 - 暖色调 */}
      <div className="fixed inset-0 pointer-events-none overflow-hidden">
        <div className="absolute -top-40 -right-40 w-96 h-96 bg-gradient-to-br from-coral/10 to-orange/10 rounded-full blur-3xl" />
        <div className="absolute top-1/3 -left-20 w-72 h-72 bg-gradient-to-br from-gold/10 to-amber-500/5 rounded-full blur-3xl" />
        <div className="absolute bottom-40 right-10 w-48 h-48 bg-gradient-to-br from-orange/10 to-coral/10 rounded-full blur-2xl" />
      </div>

      <main className="relative z-10 pb-24">
        {/* 测评中心 */}
        {activeTab === "test" && (
          <TestPage user={currentUser} />
        )}

        {/* AI 对话 */}
        {activeTab === "chat" && (
          <ChatPage
            user={currentUser}
            onFindConsultant={() => setActiveTab("consultant")}
          />
        )}

        {/* 专家咨询 - 直接嵌入（不再作为子页面） */}
        {activeTab === "consultant" && (
          <ConsultantPage onBack={() => setActiveTab("test")} />
        )}

        {/* 个人中心 */}
        {activeTab === "profile" && (
          <ProfilePage
            user={currentUser}
            onOpenReports={() => setSubPage("reports")}
            onOpenInvite={() => setSubPage("invite")}
            onOpenConsultant={() => setActiveTab("consultant")}
            onLogout={handleLogout}
          />
        )}
      </main>

      {/* 底部导航栏 */}
      <BottomNav activeTab={activeTab} onTabChange={setActiveTab} />
    </div>
  )
}

3. 高度共情和理解力
4. 认真负责，追求品质

**职业建议**
咨询顾问 | 产品经理 | 数据分析 | 教育培训 | 内容创作

💡 **建议**：完成正式的MBTI、PDP、DISC、盖洛普四大测评，获取更精准的分析结果！`,
    }
  }

  if (input.includes("生命数字") || /\d{4}[-/年]\d{1,2}[-/月]\d{1,2}/.test(input)) {
    return {
      type: "analysis",
      analysisType: "life-number",
      content: `**生命数字深度解读**

出生日期：${dateStr || "待输入"}

**主命数：7 - 智者之路**
你是天生的思考者和真理追求者。拥有敏锐的洞察力，总能看透事物的本质。

**天赋数：3 - 表达创造**
具有出色的语言天赋和创造力，无论写作、演讲还是艺术创作都能轻松驾驭。

**2026流年运势：8年 - 收获年**
过去的积累将开花结果。事业有晋升机会，财运改善，关系更加稳固。

**行动建议**
1. 把握今年的商业机会
2. 拓展高质量人脉关系
3. 平衡物质追求与精神成长`,
    }
  }

  if (input.includes("MBTI") || input.includes("性格")) {
    return {
      type: "analysis",
      analysisType: "mbti",
      content: `**MBTI 性格分析**

基于你的描述推测：**INFJ - 提倡者**
最稀有的性格类型之一，约占人口1-2%。

**认知功能栈**
1. Ni（内倾直觉）主导 - 强大的洞察力
2. Fe（外倾情感）辅助 - 深度共情能力
3. Ti（内倾思考）第三 - 逻辑分析能力

**核心优势**：深度洞察 | 使命感强 | 创造力 | 共情理解

**职业推荐**：心理咨询 | 教育培训 | 产品设计 | 内容创作

💡 建议完成正式MBTI 28题测评，获取更准确的结果！`,
    }
  }

  if (input.includes("DISC") || input.includes("行为")) {
    return {
      type: "analysis",
      analysisType: "disc",
      content: `**DISC 行为风格分析**

基于你的描述推测：**S型 + C型（稳健谨慎型）**

**S型（稳健型）特质**
- 耐心可靠，善于倾听
- 团队协作能力强
- 追求稳定和谐

**C型（谨慎型）特质**
- 注重细节和品质
- 分析能力强
- 追求完美

**沟通建议**：表达时注意节奏，适当提升决策速度

💡 建议完成正式DISC 24题测评，获取精准的行为分析！`,
    }
  }

  if (input.includes("感情") || input.includes("合盘") || input.includes("TA")) {
    return {
      type: "analysis",
      analysisType: "relationship",
      content: `**关系合盘分析**

**能量匹配度：87%**

核心契合：价值观90% | 沟通85% | 成长88%

**优势**：思想交流深度好，对未来有共同愿景
**挑战**：决策方式差异、社交需求不同

**建议**：用"我感觉..."代替"你总是..."，定期深度对话`,
    }
  }

  if (input.includes("职业") || input.includes("工作") || input.includes("天赋")) {
    return {
      type: "analysis",
      analysisType: "career",
      content: `**职业天赋分析**

**核心天赋**
1. 战略思维 ★★★★★
2. 沟通表达 ★★★★☆
3. 人际洞察 ★★★★★
4. 创新突破 ★★★★☆

**推荐方向**
第一梯队：咨询顾问 | 产品经理 | 教育培训
第二梯队：人力资源 | 内容创作 | 心理咨询

**2026职业建议**：积极参与跨领域项目，投资AI和新技能学习`,
    }
  }

  return {
    type: "text",
    content: `感谢你的提问！我可以为你提供以下分析服务：

🔮 **一键全面分析** - 综合MBTI/PDP/DISC/盖洛普多维度分析
📊 **聊天记录分析** - 上传聊天记录，AI分析性格特征
🎂 **生日解读** - 输入生日，分析生命数字和运势
🧠 **MBTI/DISC分析** - 快速性格推测

你也可以直接上传聊天记录或社交动态截图，我来帮你分析！`,
  }
}

// 初始消息
const initialMessages: Message[] = [
  {
    id: "1",
    role: "assistant",
    content: `你好！我是知己AI助手 ✨

我可以帮你：
📋 **一键分析** - 输入生日+聊天记录，AI综合分析性格
🧠 **MBTI/PDP/DISC/盖洛普** - 多维度解读
💬 **聊天记录分析** - 上传文字，推测性格类型
📊 **职业/感情** - 深度方向分析

试试输入你的生日，或者上传聊天记录开始分析吧！`,
    timestamp: new Date(),
    type: "text",
  },
]

interface ChatPageProps {
  user?: any
  onFindConsultant?: () => void
}

export function ChatPage({ user, onFindConsultant }: ChatPageProps) {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>(initialMessages)
  const [input, setInput] = useState("")
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false)
  const [showScenarios, setShowScenarios] = useState(true)
  const [showUploadPanel, setShowUploadPanel] = useState(false)
  const [uploadedText, setUploadedText] = useState("")
  const [birthday, setBirthday] = useState("")
  const [isAnalyzing, setIsAnalyzing] = useState(false)
  const messagesEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)

  // 自动滚动到底部
  const scrollToBottom = () => {
    messagesEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" })
  }

  useEffect(() => {
    scrollToBottom()
  }, [messages])

  // 发送消息
  const handleSend = async (customInput?: string) => {
    const messageText = customInput || input
    if (!messageText.trim()) return

    const userMessage: Message = {
      id: Date.now().toString(),
      role: "user",
      content: messageText,
      timestamp: new Date(),
    }

    setMessages((prev) => [...prev, userMessage])
    setInput("")
    setIsTyping(true)
    setShowScenarios(false)

    // 尝试调用后端API
    try {
      const response = await fetch("/api/analysis", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          userId: user?.id || "anonymous",
          analysisType: "comprehensive",
          birthday: birthday || undefined,
          chatlog: uploadedText || undefined,
          materials: messageText,
          name: user?.nickname || user?.name || "",
        }),
      })

      if (response.ok) {
        const data = await response.json()
        if (data.success) {
          const assistantMessage: Message = {
            id: (Date.now() + 1).toString(),
            role: "assistant",
            content: data.data.content,
            timestamp: new Date(),
            type: "analysis",
            analysisType: data.data.analysisType,
          }
          setMessages((prev) => [...prev, assistantMessage])
          setIsTyping(false)
          return
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {
      // API 失败，降级到本地模拟
      console.warn("[知己] API调用失败，使用本地模拟:", e)
    }

    // 本地模拟响应
    setTimeout(() => {
      const response = generateAnalysisResponse(messageText, birthday)
      const assistantMessage: Message = {
        id: (Date.now() + 1).toString(),
        role: "assistant",
        content: response.content,
        timestamp: new Date(),
        type: response.type as "text" | "analysis",
        analysisType: response.analysisType,
      }
      setMessages((prev) => [...prev, assistantMessage])
      setIsTyping(false)
    }, 1500)
  }

  // 一键AI分析
  const handleOneKeyAnalysis = async () => {
    setIsAnalyzing(true)
    setShowUploadPanel(false)

    let analysisContent = "请帮我做一键全面性格分析"
    if (birthday) analysisContent += `\n我的生日：${birthday}`
    if (uploadedText) analysisContent += `\n以下是我的聊天记录/材料：\n${uploadedText}`

    const userMessage: Message = {
      id: Date.now().toString(),
      role: "user",
      content: `🔮 一键AI分析\n${birthday ? `生日：${birthday}` : ""}${uploadedText ? `\n已上传材料（${uploadedText.length}字）` : ""}`,
      timestamp: new Date(),
    }
    setMessages((prev) => [...prev, userMessage])
    setIsTyping(true)
    setShowScenarios(false)

    // 调用API
    try {
      const response = await fetch("/api/analysis", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          userId: user?.id || "anonymous",
          analysisType: uploadedText ? "chatlog" : birthday ? "birthday" : "comprehensive",
          birthday: birthday || undefined,
          chatlog: uploadedText || undefined,
          name: user?.nickname || user?.name || "",
        }),
      })

      if (response.ok) {
        const data = await response.json()
        if (data.success) {
          const assistantMessage: Message = {
            id: (Date.now() + 1).toString(),
            role: "assistant",
            content: data.data.content,
            timestamp: new Date(),
            type: "analysis",
            analysisType: data.data.analysisType,
          }
          setMessages((prev) => [...prev, assistantMessage])
          setIsTyping(false)
          setIsAnalyzing(false)
          return
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn("[知己] API调用失败，使用本地模拟:", e)
    }

    // 本地降级
    setTimeout(() => {
      const response = generateAnalysisResponse(analysisContent, birthday)
      const assistantMessage: Message = {
        id: (Date.now() + 1).toString(),
        role: "assistant",
        content: response.content,
        timestamp: new Date(),
        type: "analysis",
        analysisType: response.analysisType,
      }
      setMessages((prev) => [...prev, assistantMessage])
      setIsTyping(false)
      setIsAnalyzing(false)
    }, 2000)
  }

  // 复制内容
  const handleCopy = (content: string) => {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(content)
    alert("内容已复制到剪贴板")
  }

  // 保存报告
  const handleSave = (message: Message) => {
    alert("报告已保存到「我的」-「解读报告」")
  }

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-screen bg-gradient-to-b from-background to-muted/30">
      {/* Header */}
      <header className="glass-strong px-4 py-3 safe-top sticky top-0 z-10">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="w-11 h-11 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-coral via-orange-400 to-gold flex items-center justify-center shadow-lg shadow-coral/20">
            <Sparkles className="w-5 h-5 text-white" />
          </div>
          <div className="flex-1">
            <h1 className="font-bold text-foreground">知己 AI</h1>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">一键分析 · 多维解读</p>
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
            <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">在线</span>
          </div>
          {onFindConsultant && (
            <button
              onClick={onFindConsultant}
              className="flex items-center gap-1 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl bg-coral/10 text-coral text-xs font-medium hover:bg-coral/20 transition-colors"
            >
              <Users className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
              找专家
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </header>

      {/* 一键分析入口卡片 */}
      {showScenarios && (
        <div className="px-4 py-3 space-y-3">
          {/* 一键分析 */}
          <Card
            className="glass p-4 rounded-2xl border-0 cursor-pointer hover:shadow-lg transition-all active:scale-[0.98]"
            onClick={() => setShowUploadPanel(true)}
          >
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-coral to-gold flex items-center justify-center shadow-lg">
                <Zap className="w-6 h-6 text-white" />
              </div>
              <div className="flex-1">
                <h3 className="font-bold text-foreground text-sm">一键AI全面分析</h3>
                <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">输入生日 + 上传聊天记录，AI综合分析你的性格</p>
              </div>
              <ChevronDown className="w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground" />
            </div>
          </Card>

          {/* 快速入口 */}
          <div className="flex gap-2 overflow-x-auto no-scrollbar pb-1">
            {quickScenarios.map((scenario, index) => (
              <button
                key={index}
                onClick={() => handleSend(scenario.query)}
                className="flex items-center gap-1.5 glass px-3 py-2 rounded-xl text-xs whitespace-nowrap hover:bg-coral/10 hover:text-coral transition-colors"
              >
                <scenario.icon className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                {scenario.label}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 上传面板 */}
      {showUploadPanel && (
        <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-border/50 bg-gradient-to-b from-coral/5 to-transparent">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
            <h3 className="font-semibold text-foreground text-sm flex items-center gap-1.5">
              <Zap className="w-4 h-4 text-coral" />
              一键AI分析
            </h3>
            <button onClick={() => setShowUploadPanel(false)} className="text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground">
              <X className="w-4 h-4" />
            </button>
          </div>

          {/* 生日输入 */}
          <div className="mb-3">
            <label className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1 flex items-center gap-1">
              <Calendar className="w-3 h-3" /> 出生日期（选填）
            </label>
            <input
              type="date"
              value={birthday}
              onChange={(e) => setBirthday(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full bg-muted/80 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 text-sm text-foreground focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/50"
            />
          </div>

          {/* 聊天记录/材料上传 */}
          <div className="mb-3">
            <label className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1 flex items-center gap-1">
              <FileText className="w-3 h-3" /> 聊天记录 / 材料（选填）
            </label>
            <textarea
              value={uploadedText}
              onChange={(e) => setUploadedText(e.target.value)}
              placeholder="粘贴聊天记录、朋友圈内容、或任何文字材料...&#10;AI 将分析文本中的性格特征"
              rows={4}
              className="w-full bg-muted/80 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 text-sm text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/50 resize-none"
            />
            {uploadedText && (
              <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mt-1">已输入 {uploadedText.length} 字</p>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* 开始分析按钮 */}
          <Button
            onClick={handleOneKeyAnalysis}
            disabled={isAnalyzing || (!birthday && !uploadedText)}
            className="w-full bg-gradient-to-r from-coral to-gold text-white rounded-xl py-5 shadow-lg disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {isAnalyzing ? (
              <>
                <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 mr-2 animate-spin" />
                AI分析中...
              </>
            ) : (
              <>
                <Sparkles className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                开始一键分析
              </>
            )}
          </Button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 消息列表 */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-4 space-y-4 no-scrollbar">
        {messages.map((message) => (
          <div key={message.id} className={cn("flex gap-3", message.role === "user" ? "flex-row-reverse" : "flex-row")}>
            {/* 头像 */}
            <div
              className={cn(
                "w-9 h-9 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 shadow-md",
                message.role === "user"
                  ? "bg-gradient-to-br from-teal to-cyan-400"
                  : "bg-gradient-to-br from-coral via-orange-400 to-gold",
              )}
            >
              {message.role === "user" ? (
                <UserIcon className="w-4 h-4 text-white" />
              ) : (
                <Bot className="w-4 h-4 text-white" />
              )}
            </div>

            {/* 消息内容 */}
            <div
              className={cn(
                "max-w-[85%] rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 shadow-sm",
                message.role === "user"
                  ? "bg-gradient-to-br from-teal to-cyan-400 text-white rounded-tr-md"
                  : "glass rounded-tl-md",
              )}
            >
              <div className={cn("text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap leading-relaxed", message.role === "assistant" && "text-foreground")}>
                {message.content.split("\n").map((line, i) => {
                  if (line.startsWith("**") && line.endsWith("**")) {
                    return <p key={i} className="font-bold text-foreground my-2 first:mt-0">{line.replace(/\*\*/g, "")}</p>
                  }
                  if (line.startsWith("## ")) {
                    return <p key={i} className="font-bold text-foreground my-2 first:mt-0 text-base">{line.replace("## ", "")}</p>
                  }
                  if (line.startsWith("### ")) {
                    return <p key={i} className="font-semibold text-foreground my-1.5">{line.replace("### ", "")}</p>
                  }
                  if (line.startsWith("- ") || line.startsWith("* ")) {
                    return <p key={i} className="ml-2 my-0.5">{line}</p>
                  }
                  if (line.startsWith("---")) {
                    return <hr key={i} className="my-3 border-border/50" />
                  }
                  return <p key={i} className="my-1 first:mt-0 last:mb-0">{line}</p>
                })}
              </div>

              {/* 操作按钮 */}
              {message.role === "assistant" && message.type === "analysis" && (
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1 mt-4 pt-3 border-t border-border/50">
                  <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="h-8 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-coral hover:bg-coral/10" onClick={() => handleCopy(message.content)}>
                    <Copy className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" /> 复制
                  </Button>
                  <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="h-8 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-coral hover:bg-coral/10">
                    <Share2 className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" /> 分享
                  </Button>
                  <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="h-8 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-coral hover:bg-coral/10" onClick={() => handleSave(message)}>
                    <BookmarkPlus className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" /> 保存
                  </Button>
                  <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="h-8 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-teal hover:bg-teal/10">
                    <ThumbsUp className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" /> 有用
                  </Button>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}

        {/* 正在输入 */}
        {isTyping && (
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-coral via-orange-400 to-gold flex items-center justify-center shadow-md">
              <Bot className="w-4 h-4 text-white" />
            </div>
            <div className="glass rounded-2xl rounded-tl-md px-4 py-3">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <div className="flex gap-1">
                  <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-coral rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: "0ms" }} />
                  <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-coral rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: "150ms" }} />
                  <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-coral rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: "300ms" }} />
                </div>
                <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">AI正在分析...</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* 推荐问题 */}
        {messages.length <= 2 && !showUploadPanel && (
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 pt-2">
            {suggestedQuestions.map((question, index) => (
              <button
                key={index}
                onClick={() => handleSend(question)}
                className="glass px-3 py-2 rounded-xl text-xs text-foreground hover:bg-coral/10 hover:text-coral transition-colors"
              >
                {question}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}

        <div ref={messagesEndRef} />
      </div>

      {/* 输入区域 */}
      <div className="glass-strong px-4 py-3 safe-bottom">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <button
            onClick={() => setShowUploadPanel(!showUploadPanel)}
            className={cn(
              "w-10 h-10 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center transition-colors",
              showUploadPanel ? "bg-coral/20 text-coral" : "bg-muted/80 text-muted-foreground hover:bg-coral/10 hover:text-coral"
            )}
          >
            <Upload className="w-5 h-5" />
          </button>
          <div className="flex-1 relative">
            <input
              type="text"
              value={input}
              onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
              onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === "Enter" && handleSend()}
              placeholder="输入生日或问题开始分析..."
              className="w-full bg-muted/80 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-sm text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-coral/50"
            />
          </div>
          <button
            onClick={() => handleSend()}
            disabled={!input.trim()}
            className={cn(
              "w-10 h-10 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center transition-all",
              input.trim()
                ? "bg-gradient-to-br from-coral via-orange-400 to-gold text-white shadow-lg shadow-coral/30 hover:scale-105"
                : "bg-muted/80 text-muted-foreground",
            )}
          >
            <Send className="w-5 h-5" />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/app/api/user/route.ts
  contents: /**
 * 知己 · 用户 API
 * POST /api/user - 注册/登录
 * GET /api/user?id=xxx - 获取用户信息
 * PUT /api/user - 更新用户信息
 */

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
import { connectToDatabase, COLLECTIONS } from "@/lib/mongodb"

/** POST: 注册或登录 */
export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await request.json()
    const { action, phone, password, nickname, inviteCode } = body

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    const usersCol = db.collection(COLLECTIONS.USERS)

    if (action === "register") {
      // 注册
      if (!phone || !password) {
        return NextResponse.json({ error: "手机号和密码必填" }, { status: 400 })
      }

      // 检查是否已注册
      const existing = await usersCol.findOne({ phone })
      if (existing) {
        return NextResponse.json({ error: "该手机号已注册" }, { status: 409 })
      }

      // 生成邀请码
      const newInviteCode = Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 8).toUpperCase()

      const newUser = {
        phone,
        password, // 生产环境需加密
        nickname: nickname || `用户${phone.slice(-4)}`,
        avatar: "",
        vip: false,
        vipExpireDate: null,
        points: inviteCode ? 100 : 0, // 被邀请送100积分
        inviteCode: newInviteCode,
        invitedBy: inviteCode || null,
        createdAt: new Date(),
      }

      const result = await usersCol.insertOne(newUser)

      // 给邀请人加积分
      if (inviteCode) {
        await usersCol.updateOne(
          { inviteCode },
          { $inc: { points: 200 } }
        )
      }

      return NextResponse.json({
        success: true,
        user: { ...newUser, _id: result.insertedId, id: result.insertedId.toString() },
      })
    }

    if (action === "login") {
      // 登录
      if (!phone || !password) {
        return NextResponse.json({ error: "手机号和密码必填" }, { status: 400 })
      }

      const user = await usersCol.findOne({ phone, password })
      if (!user) {
        return NextResponse.json({ error: "手机号或密码错误" }, { status: 401 })
      }

      return NextResponse.json({
        success: true,
        user: { ...user, id: user._id.toString() },
      })
    }

    return NextResponse.json({ error: "无效的 action 参数" }, { status: 400 })
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error("[知己API] 用户操作失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "服务器错误", detail: error.message }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

/** GET: 获取用户信息 */
export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const userId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get("id")
    const phone = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get("phone")

    if (!userId && !phone) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: "缺少 id 或 phone 参数" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    const query = userId ? { _id: userId } : { phone }
    const user = await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.USERS).findOne(query)

    if (!user) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: "用户不存在" }, { status: 404 })
    }

    // 不返回密码
    const { password, ...userWithoutPassword } = user as any
    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, user: { ...userWithoutPassword, id: user._id.toString() } })
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error("[知己API] 获取用户失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "服务器错误", detail: error.message }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

/** PUT: 更新用户信息 */
export async function PUT(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await request.json()
    const { userId, updates } = body

    if (!userId || !updates) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: "缺少 userId 或 updates" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    // 不允许更新敏感字段
    delete updates.password
    delete updates._id
    delete updates.inviteCode

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.USERS).updateOne(
      { _id: userId },
      { $set: { ...updates, updatedAt: new Date() } }
    )

    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, message: "用户信息已更新" })
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error("[知己API] 更新用户失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "服务器错误", detail: error.message }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

创建报告 API 路由。
[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/app/api/reports/route.ts
  contents: /**
 * 知己 · 报告 API
 * GET /api/reports?userId=xxx - 获取用户所有报告
 * POST /api/reports - 保存新报告
 * DELETE /api/reports?id=xxx - 删除报告
 */

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
import { connectToDatabase, COLLECTIONS } from "@/lib/mongodb"
import { ObjectId } from "mongodb"

/** GET: 获取用户报告列表 */
export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const userId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get("userId")

    if (!userId) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: "缺少 userId 参数" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    const reports = await db
      .collection(COLLECTIONS.REPORTS)
      .find({ userId })
      .sort({ createdAt: -1 })
      .limit(100)
      .toArray()

    return NextResponse.json({
      success: true,
      data: reports.map(r => ({ ...r, id: r._id.toString() })),
      total: reports.length,
    })
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error("[知己API] 获取报告失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "服务器错误", detail: error.message }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

/** POST: 保存报告 */
export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await request.json()
    const { userId, type, name, result } = body

    if (!userId || !type || !result) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: "缺少必要参数" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    const report = {
      userId,
      type,
      name: name || `${type} 报告`,
      result,
      isFavorite: false,
      createdAt: new Date(),
    }

    const insertResult = await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.REPORTS).insertOne(report)

    return NextResponse.json({
      success: true,
      reportId: insertResult.insertedId.toString(),
      message: "报告已保存",
    })
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error("[知己API] 保存报告失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "服务器错误", detail: error.message }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

/** DELETE: 删除报告 */
export async function DELETE(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const reportId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get("id")

    if (!reportId) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: "缺少 id 参数" }, { status: 400 })
    }

    const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
    await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.REPORTS).deleteOne({ _id: new ObjectId(reportId) })

    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, message: "报告已删除" })
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error("[知己API] 删除报告失败:", error)
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "服务器错误", detail: error.message }, { status: 500 })
  }
}

        console.warn("[知己API] 保存报告到数据库失败（继续返回结果）:", dbError)
      }
    }
  new_string:     // 保存到数据库（如果有 userId，MongoDB 不可用则跳过）
    if (userId) {
      try {
        const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
        await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.REPORTS).insertOne({
          userId,
          type: `ai-${analysisType}`,
          name: `AI${analysisType === "birthday" ? "生日" : analysisType === "chatlog" ? "聊天记录" : "综合"}分析报告`,
          result: { content: analysisResult, analysisType, inputData: { name, birthday, hasChatlog: !!chatlog } },
          createdAt: new Date(),
        })
      } catch (dbError: any) {
        // MongoDB 不可用时静默跳过，不影响返回结果
        console.warn("[知己API] 保存报告到数据库失败（跳过）:", dbError?.message || dbError)
      }
    }

> 上限50条，超过则整合相似条目

---

## 2026-02-10

### 1. 四大测试题库构建
**问题**：需要为MBTI/PDP/DISC/盖洛普创建完整的测试题库
**解决方案**：
- MBTI：28题版本（4维度×7题），比标准93题精简但覆盖完整
- PDP：30题（5类型×6题），5分制评分
- DISC：24题（4类型×6题），5分制评分，答案值包含类型前缀（如D5/I3）
- 盖洛普：20题（4领域×5题），二选一快速判断
**关键步骤**：创建 `lib/test-questions.ts` 统一管理题库、计算逻辑、类型详解

### 2. 测试页面组件设计
**问题**：需要一个完整的测试流程（列表→介绍→答题→加载→结果）
**解决方案**：使用状态机模式管理5个步骤（list/intro/testing/loading/result）
**关键点**：
- 答题后自动跳转下一题（300ms延迟提供视觉反馈）
- 支持返回上一题修改答案
- 进度条动态显示
- 结果页展示维度得分可视化

### 3. AI对话页增强
**问题**：需要支持一键分析、材料上传、聊天记录分析
**解决方案**：
- 新增上传面板（生日输入+聊天记录文本框）
- 优先调用 /api/analysis API，失败时降级到本地模拟
- API支持3种分析类型：birthday、chatlog、comprehensive
**关键点**：前端→API→AI服务→数据库的完整链路，任一环节失败都有降级方案

### 4. MongoDB 连接与优雅降级
**问题**：MongoDB不一定随时可用，不能阻塞前端
**解决方案**：
- 连接超时设为3秒（原5秒太长）
- API中MongoDB操作用try-catch包裹，失败不影响响应
- 前端fetch API失败时降级到本地模拟数据
**关键配置**：`connectTimeoutMS: 3000, serverSelectionTimeoutMS: 3000`

### 5. 底部导航重构
**问题**：从3Tab(首页/知己/我的)重构为4Tab(测评/知己/专家/我的)
**解决方案**：
- 类型从 `"home" | "chat" | "profile"` 改为 `"test" | "chat" | "consultant" | "profile"`
- 专家从子页面提升为主Tab
- 知己(AI对话)保留中央浮起按钮设计
- 导出 TabType 类型供 page.tsx 使用

### 6. Next.js API Routes 最佳实践
**经验**：
- 路由文件放在 `app/api/xxx/route.ts`
- 使用 `NextRequest` 和 `NextResponse`
- POST用 `request.json()` 获取body
- GET用 `request.nextUrl.searchParams` 获取参数
- MongoDB ObjectId 需要从 `mongodb` 包导入

---

## 经验速查表

| 场景 | 方案 |
|:---|:---|
| 测试题库设计 | 统一类型定义 + calculateResult 函数 |
| 多步骤流程 | 状态机模式（state: "list"/"intro"/"testing"等） |
| API降级 | try-catch + 本地模拟数据兜底 |
| MongoDB连接 | 缩短超时 + 全局缓存 + 优雅降级 |
| 底部导航扩展 | 导出TabType类型 + page.tsx统一管理 |

## 路由架构

知己当前采用**单页应用（SPA）状态路由**，在 `app/page.tsx` 中通过 `activeTab` 状态控制页面切换。

```
app/page.tsx → activeTab 状态（4Tab）
├── "test"       → <TestPage />          components/test-page.tsx
├── "chat"       → <ChatPage />          components/chat-page.tsx
├── "consultant" → <ConsultantPage />    components/consultant-page.tsx
└── "profile"    → <ProfilePage />       components/profile-page.tsx

子页面（通过 subPage 状态控制）
├── "reports"    → <ReportsPage />       components/reports-page.tsx
└── "invite"     → <InvitePage />        components/invite-page.tsx
```

## API 路由

```
app/api/
├── analysis/route.ts   → POST: AI分析（生日/聊天记录/综合）
├── test/route.ts       → POST: 保存测试记录 / GET: 获取记录
├── user/route.ts       → POST: 注册/登录 / GET: 查询 / PUT: 更新
└── reports/route.ts    → GET: 报告列表 / POST: 保存 / DELETE: 删除
```

## 底部导航结构

```
┌──────────┬──────────┬──────────┬──────────┐
│   测评   │         知己         │   专家   │   我的   │
│  (test)  │  (chat) [中央浮起]  │(consult) │(profile) │
└──────────┴──────────┴──────────┴──────────┘
```

/**
 * 知己 · 底部导航栏
 * 四个Tab：首页、知己AI(AI对话)、专家、我的
 */

import { Home, User, MessageCircle, Sparkles, Users } from "lucide-react"
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

export type TabType = "home" | "chat" | "consultant" | "profile"

interface BottomNavProps {
  activeTab: TabType
  onTabChange: (tab: TabType) => void
}

export function BottomNav({ activeTab, onTabChange }: BottomNavProps) {
  return (
    <nav className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 z-50 safe-bottom">
      <div className="mx-4 mb-2">
        <div className="glass rounded-2xl shadow-xl shadow-black/5">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-around py-2 px-2">
            {/* 首页 */}
            <button
              onClick={() => onTabChange("home")}
              className={cn(
                "flex flex-col items-center gap-1 px-4 py-2 rounded-xl transition-all duration-300",
                activeTab === "home" ? "text-coral scale-105" : "text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground",
              )}
            >
              <Home className="w-5 h-5" strokeWidth={activeTab === "home" ? 2.5 : 2} />
              <span className="text-xs font-medium">首页</span>
            </button>

            {/* 知己AI - 中央按钮 */}
            <button onClick={() => onTabChange("chat")} className="relative -mt-8">
              <div
                className={cn(
                  "w-16 h-16 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center shadow-xl transition-all duration-300",
                  "bg-gradient-to-br from-coral via-orange to-gold",
                  activeTab === "chat"
                    ? "scale-110 shadow-coral/40 ring-4 ring-coral/20"
                    : "shadow-coral/25 hover:scale-105",
                )}
              >
                <div className="relative">
                  <MessageCircle className="w-7 h-7 text-white" strokeWidth={2.5} />
                  <Sparkles className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-white absolute -top-1 -right-1 animate-pulse" />
                </div>
              </div>
              <span
                className={cn(
                  "absolute -bottom-5 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 text-xs font-bold whitespace-nowrap",
                  activeTab === "chat" ? "text-coral" : "text-muted-foreground",
                )}
              >
                知己AI
              </span>
            </button>

            {/* 专家 */}
            <button
              onClick={() => onTabChange("consultant")}
              className={cn(
                "flex flex-col items-center gap-1 px-4 py-2 rounded-xl transition-all duration-300",
                activeTab === "consultant" ? "text-coral scale-105" : "text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground",
              )}
            >
              <Users className="w-5 h-5" strokeWidth={activeTab === "consultant" ? 2.5 : 2} />
              <span className="text-xs font-medium">专家</span>
            </button>

            {/* 我的 */}
            <button
              onClick={() => onTabChange("profile")}
              className={cn(
                "flex flex-col items-center gap-1 px-4 py-2 rounded-xl transition-all duration-300",
                activeTab === "profile" ? "text-coral scale-105" : "text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground",
              )}
            >
              <User className="w-5 h-5" strokeWidth={activeTab === "profile" ? 2.5 : 2} />
              <span className="text-xs font-medium">我的</span>
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </nav>
  )

现在更新主路由 `page.tsx`（tab名称变更）和重构首页（原测评页→首页，增加slogan + 数字能量模块 + 分享按钮）：
[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/app/page.tsx
  contents: "use client"

/**
 * 知己 · 主入口页面
 * 四Tab路由：首页(home) → 知己AI(chat) → 专家(consultant) → 我的(profile)
 * 子页面：报告中心、发起人驾驶舱
 */

import { useState, useEffect } from "react"
import { BottomNav, type TabType } from "@/components/bottom-nav"
import { HomePage } from "@/components/home-page"
import { ChatPage } from "@/components/chat-page"
import { ProfilePage } from "@/components/profile-page"
import { ReportsPage } from "@/components/reports-page"
import { InvitePage } from "@/components/invite-page"
import { ConsultantPage } from "@/components/consultant-page"
import { userDB, type User } from "@/lib/local-db"

// 子页面类型
type SubPage = "reports" | "invite" | null

export default function App() {
  // 主Tab状态
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<TabType>("home")
  // 子页面状态
  const [subPage, setSubPage] = useState<SubPage>(null)
  // 当前用户
  const [currentUser, setCurrentUser] = useState<User>({
    id: "default_user",
    phone: "13800138000",
    password: "",
    nickname: "知己用户",
    avatar: "",
    vip: false,
    points: 100,
    inviteCode: "ZHIJI01",
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  })

  // 初始化：加载用户数据
  useEffect(() => {
    const user = userDB.getCurrentUser()
    if (user) {
      setCurrentUser(user)
    }
  }, [])

  // 退出登录
  const handleLogout = () => {
    userDB.logout()
    setCurrentUser({
      id: "default_user",
      phone: "13800138000",
      password: "",
      nickname: "知己用户",
      avatar: "",
      vip: false,
      points: 100,
      inviteCode: "ZHIJI01",
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    })
  }

  // ============ 子页面渲染 ============
  if (subPage === "reports") {
    return <ReportsPage user={currentUser} onBack={() => setSubPage(null)} />
  }
  if (subPage === "invite") {
    return <InvitePage user={currentUser} onBack={() => setSubPage(null)} />
  }

  // ============ 主页面渲染 ============
  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-50 via-white to-amber-50 relative overflow-hidden">
      {/* 背景装饰 */}
      <div className="fixed inset-0 pointer-events-none overflow-hidden">
        <div className="absolute -top-40 -right-40 w-96 h-96 bg-gradient-to-br from-coral/10 to-orange/10 rounded-full blur-3xl" />
        <div className="absolute top-1/3 -left-20 w-72 h-72 bg-gradient-to-br from-gold/10 to-amber-500/5 rounded-full blur-3xl" />
        <div className="absolute bottom-40 right-10 w-48 h-48 bg-gradient-to-br from-orange/10 to-coral/10 rounded-full blur-2xl" />
      </div>

      <main className="relative z-10 pb-24">
        {/* 首页（原测评页，增加slogan+数字能量） */}
        {activeTab === "home" && (
          <HomePage user={currentUser} onStartChat={() => setActiveTab("chat")} />
        )}

        {/* 知己AI 对话 */}
        {activeTab === "chat" && (
          <ChatPage
            user={currentUser}
            onFindConsultant={() => setActiveTab("consultant")}
          />
        )}

        {/* 专家咨询 */}
        {activeTab === "consultant" && (
          <ConsultantPage onBack={() => setActiveTab("home")} />
        )}

        {/* 个人中心 */}
        {activeTab === "profile" && (
          <ProfilePage
            user={currentUser}
            onOpenReports={() => setSubPage("reports")}
            onOpenInvite={() => setSubPage("invite")}
            onOpenConsultant={() => setActiveTab("consultant")}
            onLogout={handleLogout}
          />
        )}
      </main>

      <BottomNav activeTab={activeTab} onTabChange={setActiveTab} />
    </div>
  )
}
