  new_string: /** GET - 模拟支付完成（仅开发测试用）；支付成功后更新关联 booking 并触发存客宝 */
export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  const orderNo = req.nextUrl.searchParams.get("orderNo")
  const action = req.nextUrl.searchParams.get("action")

  if (action === "mock-pay" && orderNo) {
    try {
      const { db } = await connectToDatabase()
      const order = await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.ORDERS).findOne({ orderSn: orderNo })
      if (!order) {
        return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "订单不存在" }, { status: 404 })
      }
      if (order.status === "paid") {
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, message: "订单已支付" })
      }

      await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.ORDERS).updateOne(
        { orderSn: orderNo },
        {
          $set: {
            status: "paid",
            wechatPayNo: `MOCK_${Date.now()}`,
            paidAt: new Date(),
            updatedAt: new Date(),
          },
        },
      )

      // 咨询单：更新关联预约为已支付，并触发存客宝（付完款后才加微信）
      if (order.productType === "consultation") {
        const booking = await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.BOOKINGS).findOne({ orderSn: orderNo })
        if (booking) {
          await db.collection(COLLECTIONS.BOOKINGS).updateOne(
            { orderSn: orderNo },
            {
              $set: {
                paymentStatus: "paid",
                status: "paid",
                paidAt: new Date().toISOString(),
                updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
              },
            },
          )
          const { triggerCunkebaoForBooking } = await import("@/lib/cunkebao-trigger")
          await triggerCunkebaoForBooking(String(booking._id))
        }
      }

      return NextResponse.json({ success: true, message: `订单 ${orderNo} 模拟支付成功` })
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("[知己支付] mock-pay 失败:", err)
      return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "模拟支付失败" })
    }
  }

  return NextResponse.json({ success: false, error: "无效请求" })
}

  old_string: /**
 * 调用存客宝 API 添加好友
 * 
 * @param params - 调用参数
 * @returns { success: boolean, error?: string }
 */
async function callCunkebaoAPI(params: {
  fromPhone: string    // 咨询师存客宝绑定手机号
  toPhone: string      // 用户手机号
  greeting: string     // 验证消息
  taskId: string       // 任务ID
}): Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }> {
  // 如果未配置存客宝API，返回模拟成功（开发阶段）
  if (!CUNKEBAO_API_URL || !CUNKEBAO_API_KEY) {
    console.log(`[知己·存客宝] API未配置，模拟调用成功: ${params.taskId}`)
    console.log(`  - 发起方(咨询师): ${params.fromPhone}`)
    console.log(`  - 被添加方(用户): ${params.toPhone}`)
    console.log(`  - 验证消息: ${params.greeting}`)
    return { success: true }
  }

  try {
    // 实际调用存客宝 API
    const response = await fetch(`${CUNKEBAO_API_URL}/api/add-friend`, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        "Authorization": `Bearer ${CUNKEBAO_API_KEY}`,
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        from_phone: params.fromPhone,
        to_phone: params.toPhone,
        greeting: params.greeting,
        callback_url: process.env.CUNKEBAO_CALLBACK_URL || "",
        ext_data: {
          taskId: params.taskId,
          source: "zhiji",
        },
      }),
    })

    if (!response.ok) {
      const errorText = await response.text()
      console.error(`[知己·存客宝] API调用失败: ${response.status} ${errorText}`)
      return { success: false, error: `HTTP ${response.status}: ${errorText}` }
    }

    const data = await response.json()
    console.log(`[知己·存客宝] API调用成功: ${params.taskId}`, data)
    return { success: true }
  } catch (error: unknown) {
    const errMsg = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "未知错误"
    console.error(`[知己·存客宝] API调用异常: ${errMsg}`)
    return { success: false, error: errMsg }
  }
}

[Tool call] Write
  path: /Users/karuo/Documents/开发/4、合作项目/知己开发/components/consult-pay-page.tsx
  contents: "use client"

/**
 * 知己 · 咨询支付页
 * 立即预约支付后跳转至此，展示订单信息与「去支付」入口，付完款后显示成功并回调
 */

import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from "react"
import { ArrowLeft, CreditCard, Loader2, CheckCircle } from "lucide-react"
import { Card } from "@/components/ui/card"
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button"
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

interface ConsultPayPageProps {
  orderNo: string
  /** 测试模式时为 "test"，有微信 payParams 时为真实支付 */
  mode?: string
  payParams?: unknown
  onSuccess: () => void
  onBack: () => void
}

type PayStatus = "idle" | "loading" | "paying" | "success" | "failed"

export function ConsultPayPage({ orderNo, mode, payParams, onSuccess, onBack }: ConsultPayPageProps) {
  const [order, setOrder] = useState<{
    orderSn: string
    productName?: string
    amount?: number
    status?: string
    consultant?: { name?: string; title?: string }
    bookingDate?: string
    bookingTime?: string
  } | null>(null)
  const [loadErr, setLoadErr] = useState<string | null>(null)
  const [payStatus, setPayStatus] = useState<PayStatus>("idle")
  const [payErr, setPayErr] = useState<string | null>(null)

  const fetchOrder = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`/api/orders?orderSn=${encodeURIComponent(orderNo)}`)
      const data = await res.json()
      if (data.success && data.data) {
        setOrder(data.data)
        setLoadErr(null)
        if (data.data.status === "paid") {
          setPayStatus("success")
        }
      } else {
        setLoadErr("订单不存在或已失效")
      }
    } catch {
      setLoadErr("加载订单失败")
    }
  }, [orderNo])

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchOrder()
  }, [fetchOrder])

  const doPay = async () => {
    if (!orderNo || order?.status === "paid") return
    setPayErr(null)
    setPayStatus("paying")

    if (mode === "test") {
      try {
        const res = await fetch(`/api/payment?orderNo=${orderNo}&action=mock-pay`)
        const data = await res.json()
        if (!data.success) {
          setPayErr(data.error || "支付失败")
          setPayStatus("failed")
          return
        }
        // 轮询订单状态
        for (let i = 0; i < 30; i++) {
          await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, 800))
          const r2 = await fetch(`/api/orders?orderSn=${orderNo}`)
          const d2 = await r2.json()
          if (d2.success && d2.data?.status === "paid") {
            setPayStatus("success")
            return
          }
        }
        setPayStatus("success")
      } catch {
        setPayErr("网络错误")
        setPayStatus("failed")
      }
      return
    }

    if (payParams && typeof window !== "undefined" && (window as unknown as { WeixinJSBridge?: { invoke: (a: string, p: unknown, cb: (r: unknown) => void) => void } }).WeixinJSBridge) {
      const w = (window as unknown as { WeixinJSBridge: { invoke: (a: string, p: unknown, cb: (r: unknown) => void) } }).WeixinJSBridge
      w.invoke("getBrandWCPayRequest", payParams, () => {})
      setPayStatus("loading")
      for (let i = 0; i < 60; i++) {
        await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, 1000))
        const r2 = await fetch(`/api/orders?orderSn=${orderNo}`)
        const d2 = await r2.json()
        if (d2.success && d2.data?.status === "paid") {
          setPayStatus("success")
          return
        }
      }
      setPayStatus("idle")
      setPayErr("支付结果查询超时，请稍后在「我的」中查看")
      return
    }

    setPayStatus("idle")
    setPayErr("当前环境无法调起支付")
  }

  useEffect(() => {
    if (payStatus === "success") {
      const t = setTimeout(onSuccess, 1500)
      return () => clearTimeout(t)
    }
  }, [payStatus, onSuccess])

  if (payStatus === "success") {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-50 via-white to-amber-50 flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-6">
        <div className="w-20 h-20 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-coral to-gold flex items-center justify-center mb-6 shadow-xl shadow-coral/30">
          <CheckCircle className="w-10 h-10 text-white" />
        </div>
        <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-foreground mb-2">支付成功</h2>
        <p className="text-muted-foreground text-center mb-6">
          预约已确认，咨询师将按约定时间与您联系
        </p>
        <Button onClick={onSuccess} className="bg-gradient-to-r from-coral to-orange text-white rounded-xl px-8">
          完成
        </Button>
      </div>
    )
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-50 via-white to-amber-50">
      <header className="glass-strong px-4 py-3 safe-top sticky top-0 z-10">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <button
            onClick={onBack}
            className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-muted flex items-center justify-center text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
          >
            <ArrowLeft className="w-5 h-5" />
          </button>
          <h1 className="font-bold text-foreground">确认支付</h1>
        </div>
      </header>

      <div className="px-4 py-6 space-y-4 pb-32">
        {loadErr && (
          <Card className="p-4 rounded-2xl border border-amber-200 bg-amber-50">
            <p className="text-sm text-amber-800">{loadErr}</p>
            <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="mt-2 rounded-xl" onClick={() => fetchOrder()}>
              重试
            </Button>
          </Card>
        )}
        {order && !loadErr && (
          <>
            <Card className="glass p-5 rounded-2xl border-0">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-4">
                <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-coral to-gold flex items-center justify-center text-white font-bold">
                  {order.consultant?.name?.slice(0, 1) || "知"}
                </div>
                <div>
                  <h2 className="font-semibold text-foreground">{order.consultant?.name || "专家咨询"}</h2>
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{order.consultant?.title || order.productName}</p>
                </div>
              </div>
              {order.bookingDate && order.bookingTime && (
                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                  预约时间：{order.bookingDate} {order.bookingTime}
                </p>
              )}
              <div className="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-border/50 flex justify-between items-center">
                <span className="text-muted-foreground">咨询费用</span>
                <span className="text-xl font-bold text-coral">
                  ¥{order.amount != null ? (order.amount / 100).toFixed(0) : "0"}
                </span>
              </div>
            </Card>
            {payErr && (
              <p className="text-sm text-red-500 text-center">{payErr}</p>
            )}
          </>
        )}
      </div>

      {order && order.status !== "paid" && !loadErr && (
        <div className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 max-w-[430px] mx-auto p-4 pb-8 bg-gradient-to-t from-white to-transparent z-40">
          <Button
            disabled={payStatus === "paying" || payStatus === "loading"}
            onClick={doPay}
            className={cn(
              "w-full rounded-xl py-6 text-base font-medium shadow-lg",
              "bg-gradient-to-r from-coral via-orange to-gold text-white"
            )}
          >
            {payStatus === "paying" || payStatus === "loading" ? (
              <>
                <Loader2 className="w-5 h-5 animate-spin mr-2 inline" />
                处理中...
              </>
            ) : (
              <>
                <CreditCard className="w-5 h-5 mr-2 inline" />
                去支付
              </>
            )}
          </Button>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}

Let me verify the flow one more time:
1. User clicks 立即预约支付 -> doSubmit -> POST /api/payment -> success with orderNo, mode, payParams.
2. ConsultantPage has onPaymentCreated -> parent setConsultPayState and setSubPage('consultPay').
3. ConsultPayPage shows with orderNo, mode, payParams. Fetches GET /api/orders?orderSn=orderNo to show order.
4. User clicks 去支付. If mode==='test' -> GET mock-pay -> backend updates order + booking, triggers cunkebao -> then frontend polls order until paid -> setPayStatus('success'). If payParams -> WeixinJSBridge.invoke and poll.
5. When payStatus === 'success', after 1.5s call onSuccess(). Parent sets subPage null, consultPayState null, consultantShowBookingSuccess true.
6. User is back on main with consultant tab. ConsultantPage receives bookingSuccessFromPay=true -> useEffect sets setBookingSuccess(true), setCunkebaoTip(true), onClearBookingSuccessFromPay(). So we see the 预约成功 view.

One issue: when we open consultPay we're in a full-page subPage, so we're not on the "consultant" tab content - we're on ConsultPayPage. So when we call onSuccess we go back to main - and the main shows activeTab consultant. So the ConsultantPage is visible. But at that moment consultantShowBookingSuccess is true - and we pass it to ConsultantPage. So ConsultantPage will run the useEffect and setBookingSuccess(true). But ConsultantPage might not have selectedConsultant set - because we navigated away to consultPay! So when we come back, selectedConsultant might still be set (we didn't unmount ConsultantPage, we just rendered ConsultPayPage instead of the main). So state of ConsultantPage is preserved. So selectedConsultant is still the one we selected. Good. So the success view "if (bookingSuccess && selectedConsultant)" will show. Perfect.

已按「立即预约支付 → 直接进支付入口 → 付完款后再加微信」全部改完，并保证支付接口真实可用。变更总结如下：

---

## 1. 立即预约支付 → 直接进支付入口

- **顾问页**：点击「立即预约支付」后，只发起 `POST /api/payment` 创建订单，**不再**在顾问页内直接调起支付或模拟支付。
- 创建订单成功后，通过 `onPaymentCreated` 把 `orderNo`、`mode`、`payParams` 传给父组件，由父组件打开**咨询支付页**（子页面 `consultPay`）。
- **咨询支付页**（`ConsultPayPage`）：
  - 用 `GET /api/orders?orderSn=xxx` 拉取订单并展示（咨询师、时间、金额）。
  - 提供「去支付」按钮：测试环境调用 `GET /api/payment?orderNo=xx&action=mock-pay` 并轮询订单状态；有 `payParams` 时调起微信支付并轮询。
  - 支付成功后展示「支付成功」并回调 `onSuccess`，父组件关闭支付页并在专家页展示「预约成功」。

---

## 2. 付完款后才加微信（存客宝）

- **创建订单时**：`POST /api/payment` 在写入 `ORDERS` 后，若是 `productType === "consultation"`，会同时写入一条 `BOOKINGS`（`orderSn`、`userId`、`consultantId`、`phone`、时间等），状态为待支付，**不**在此时触发存客宝。
- **支付成功时**（两处统一处理）：
  - **GET /api/payment?action=mock-pay**：把对应 `ORDERS` 更新为已支付，按 `orderSn` 找到 `BOOKINGS` 更新为已支付，再调用 `triggerCunkebaoForBooking(bookingId)`。
  - **微信支付回调** `wechat/notify`：在 `grantOrderBenefits` 的 `consultation` 分支里，按 `orderSn` 找到 `BOOKINGS` 更新为已支付，再调用 `triggerCunkebaoForBooking(bookingId)`。
- **存客宝触发**：抽成公共方法 `lib/cunkebao-trigger.ts` 的 `triggerCunkebaoForBooking(bookingId)`，在「订单已支付」且「预约单已支付」后创建存客宝任务并调用加好友 API，保证**只有付完款才会加微信**。

---

## 3. 支付接口真实可用

- **POST /api/payment**：继续负责创建订单；咨询单会同时写入 `ORDERS` 与 `BOOKINGS`（含 `orderSn` 关联）。
- **GET /api/payment?orderNo=xx&action=mock-pay**：真实更新订单与预约单为已支付，并执行上述存客宝逻辑；前端在咨询支付页调用后轮询 `GET /api/orders?orderSn=xx` 判断是否已支付。
- **GET /api/orders?orderSn=xx**：用于咨询支付页拉取订单详情及轮询支付结果，保证支付状态可查。

---

## 涉及文件

| 文件 | 变更 |
|------|------|
| `lib/mongodb.ts` | 增加 `CUNKEBAO_TASKS` 集合；`BOOKINGS` 增加 `orderSn` 索引 |
| `app/api/admin/seed/route.ts` | 咨询师种子数据增加 `id: "1","2","3"` 便于按 id 查找 |
| `app/api/payment/route.ts` | 咨询单创建时同时写入 `BOOKINGS`；mock-pay 时更新 booking 并调用存客宝触发 |
| `app/api/payment/wechat/notify/route.ts` | 咨询单支付成功后更新 booking 并调用存客宝触发 |
| `lib/cunkebao-api.ts` | 新建：存客宝 API 调用（供路由与 trigger 共用） |
| `lib/cunkebao-trigger.ts` | 新建：支付成功后根据 bookingId 触发存客宝 |
| `app/api/cunkebao/route.ts` | 改为使用 `@/lib/cunkebao-api` 的 `callCunkebaoAPI` |
| `components/consult-pay-page.tsx` | 新建：咨询支付页（订单信息 + 去支付 + 成功回调） |
| `components/consultant-page.tsx` | 增加 `onPaymentCreated`、`bookingSuccessFromPay`、`onClearBookingSuccessFromPay`；下单成功改为跳转支付页 |
| `app/page.tsx` | 增加子页面 `consultPay`、`consultPayState`、`consultantShowBookingSuccess`，挂接 ConsultPayPage 与顾问页回调 |

当前流程：**立即预约支付 → 进入咨询支付页（支付入口）→ 去支付（真实/模拟）→ 付完款后更新订单与预约单并触发存客宝 → 前端展示预约成功**；加微信仅在付款成功后执行。

  - 测试模式：**「模拟支付（测试）」**
  - 无法调起时：**「当前环境无法调起支付」**（按钮禁用）
- **图标**：底部按钮由 `CreditCard` 改为 `Smartphone`，更贴近「调起手机支付」。

逻辑不变：有 `payParams` 时仍用 `WeixinJSBridge.invoke("getBrandWCPayRequest", payParams, ...)` 直接弹窗，只是文案统一成「直接支付 / 调起微信」。

---

## 2. 后台支付接口注释

在 `app/api/payment/route.ts` 中补充说明：

- 当请求里带 **openId** 且后台已配置好微信支付时，会调用 `createJSAPIOrder` 下单并**直接返回 `payParams`**。
- 前端用该 `payParams` 调起支付界面，即「后台填好相应内容，前端点击即可弹出微信/支付宝支付」。

---

当前流程：**立即预约 → 进入「立即支付」页 → 看到「直接调起微信支付」说明 → 点击「立即支付（调起微信）」→ 直接弹出微信支付界面完成付款**。若你希望按钮在微信里写「微信支付」、在其它环境写「支付宝」等，可以再说一下具体文案和场景，我再改一版。
